Both of\n261:       //    these operations are relatively rare and the read lock is held for a short period\n262:       //    of time.\n263:       //\n264:       // TODO(mattklein123): Right now the dynamic forward proxy / DNS cache works similar to how\n265:       //                     logical DNS works, meaning that we only store a single address per\n266:       //                     resolution. \n527: void HostImpl::weight(uint32_t new_weight) { weight_ = std::max(1U, new_weight); }\n528: \n529: std::vector<HostsPerLocalityConstSharedPtr> HostsPerLocalityImpl::filter(\n530:     const std::vector<std::function<bool(const Host&)>>& predicates) const {\n531:   // We keep two lists: one for being able to mutate the clone and one for returning to the\n532:   // caller. Creating them both at the start avoids iterating over the mutable values at the end\n533:   // to convert them to a const pointer.\n534:   std::vector<std::shared_ptr<HostsPerLocalityImpl>> mutable_clones;\n535:   std::vector<HostsPerLocalityConstSharedPtr> filtered_clones;\n536: \n537:   mutable_clones.reserve(predicates.size());\n538:   filtered_clones.reserve(predicates.size());\n539:   for (size_t i = 0; i < predicates.size(); ++i) {\n540:     mutable_clones.emplace_back(std::make_shared<HostsPerLocalityImpl>());\n541:     filtered_clones.emplace_back(mutable_clones.back());\n542:     mutable_clones.back()->local_ = local_;\n543:   }\n544: \n545:   for (const auto& hosts_locality : hosts_per_locality_) {\n546:     std::vector<HostVector> current_locality_hosts;\n547:     current_locality_hosts.resize(predicates.size());\n548: \n549:     // Since # of hosts >> # of predicates, we iterate over the hosts in the outer loop.\n550:     for (const auto& host : hosts_locality) {\n551:       for (size_t i = 0; i < predicates.size(); ++i) {\n552:         if (predicates[i](*host)) {\n553:           current_locality_hosts[i].emplace_back(host);\n554:         }\n555:       }\n556:     }\n557: \n558:     for (size_t i = 0; i < predicates.size(); ++i) {\n559:       mutable_clones[i]->hosts_per_locality_.push_back(std::move(current_locality_hosts[i]));\n560:     }\n561:   }\n562: \n563:   return filtered_clones;\n564: }\n565: \n566: void HostSetImpl::updateHosts(PrioritySet::UpdateHostsParams&& update_hosts_params,\n567: HostSetImpl::rebuildLocalityScheduler(\n602:     std::unique_ptr<EdfScheduler<LocalityEntry>>& locality_scheduler,\n603:     std::vector<std::shared_ptr<LocalityEntry>>& locality_entries,\n604:     const HostsPerLocality& eligible_hosts_per_locality, const HostVector& eligible_hosts,\n605:     HostsPerLocalityConstSharedPtr all_hosts_per_locality,\n606:     HostsPerLocalityConstSharedPtr excluded_hosts_per_locality,\n607:     LocalityWeightsConstSharedPtr locality_weights, uint32_t overprovisioning_factor) {\n608:   // Rebuild the locality scheduler by computing the effective weight of each\n609:   // locality in this priority. The scheduler is reset by default, and is rebuilt only if we have\n610:   // locality weights (i.e. using EDS) and there is at least one eligible host in this priority.\n611:   //\n612:   // We omit building a scheduler when there are zero eligible hosts in the priority as\n613:   // all the localities will have zero effective weight. At selection time, we'll either select\n614:   // from a different scheduler or there will be no available hosts in the priority. At that point\n615:   // we'll rely on other mechanisms such as panic mode to select a host, none of which rely on the\n616:   // scheduler.\n617:   //\n618:   // TODO(htuch): if the underlying locality index ->\n619:   // envoy::config::core::v3::Locality hasn't changed in hosts_/healthy_hosts_/degraded_hosts_, we\n620:   // could just update locality_weight_ without rebuilding. Similar to how host\n621:   // level WRR works, we would age out the existing entries via picks and lazily\n622:   // apply the new weights.\n623:   locality_scheduler = nullptr;\n624:   if (all_hosts_per_locality != nullptr && locality_weights != nullptr &&\n625:       !locality_weights->empty() && !eligible_hosts.empty()) {\n626:     locality_scheduler = std::make_unique<EdfScheduler<LocalityEntry>>();\n627:     locality_entries.clear();\n628:     for (uint32_t i = 0; i < all_hosts_per_locality->get().size(); ++i) {\n629:       const double effective_weight = effectiveLocalityWeight(\n630:           i, eligible_hosts_per_locality, *excluded_hosts_per_locality, *all_hosts_per_locality,\n631:           *locality_weights, overprovisioning_factor);\n632:       if (effective_weight > 0) {\n633:         locality_entries.emplace_back(std::make_shared<LocalityEntry>(i, effective_weight));\n634:         locality_scheduler->add(effective_weight, locality_entries.back());\n635:       }\n636:     }\n637:     // If all effective weights were zero, reset the scheduler.\n638:     if (locality_scheduler->empty()) {\n639:       locality_scheduler = nullptr;\n640:     }\n641:   }\n642: }\n643: \n644: absl::optional<uint32_t> HostSetImpl::chooseHealthyLocality() {\n645:   return chooseLocality(healthy_locality_scheduler_.get());\n646: }\n647: \n648: absl::optional<uint32_t> HostSetImpl::chooseDegradedLocality() {\n649:   return      const HostsPerLocality& excluded_hosts_per_locality,\n710:                                             const HostsPerLocality& all_hosts_per_locality,\n711:    return true;\n2365:           }\n2366:           return false;\n2367:         });\n2368:     current_priority_hosts.erase(erase_from, current_priority_hosts.end());\n2369:   }\n2370: \n2371:   // ASSERT(parent_.main_thread_dispatcher_.isThreadSafe());\n\n  const std::chrono::steady_clock::duration now_duration =\n emplaced_host;\n  {\n    absl::WriterMutexLock lock{&host_map_lock_};\n\n    // NOTE: Right now we allow a DNS cache to be shared between multiple clusters. Though we have\n    // connection/request circuit breakers on the cluster, we don't have any way to control the\n    // maximum hosts on a cluster. We currently assume that host data shared via shared pointer is\n    // a marginal memory cost above that already used by connections and requests, so relying on\n    // connection/request circuit breakers is sufficient. host_map_it->second.logical_host_->address()->asString(),\n                host_info->address()->asString());\n\n      // Remove the old host.\n      hosts_removed.emplace_back(host_map_it->second.logical_host_);\n      host_map_.erase(host_map_it);\n\n      // Create and add the new host with the updated address.\n      emplaced_host = lb_factory_->create(lb_params_); }\n\n  Upstream::MockLoadBalancerContext* setHostAndReturnContext(const std::string& host) {\n    downstream_headers_.remove(\":authority\");\n StreamInfo::StreamSharingMayImpactPooling::SharedWithUpstreamConnection);\n\n    return &lb_context_;\n  }\n\n  void setOutlierFailed(const std::string& host) {\n    for (auto& h : cluster_->prioritySet().hostSetsPerPriority()[0]->hosts()) {\n      if (h->hostname() == host) {\n        h->healthFlagSet(Upstream::Host::HealthFlag::FAILED_OUTLIER_CHECK);\n        break;\n      }\n    }\n  }\n\n  void clearOutlierFailed(const std::string& host) {\n    for (auto& h : cluster_->prioritySet().hostSetsPerPriority()[0]->hosts()) {\n      if (h->hostname() == host) {\n        h->healthFlagClear(Upstream::Host::HealthFlag::FAILED_OUTLIER_CHECK);\n        break;\n      }\n    }\n  }\n\n  MOCK_METHOD(void, onMemberUpdateCb,\n              (const Upstream::HostVector& \"fake_cluster_name\";\n  const std::string host = \"localhost\";\n  const int port = 80;\n  std::pair<bool, absl::optional<envoy::config::cluster::v3::Cluster>> sub_cluster_pair =\n      cluster_->createSubClusterConfig(cluster_name, host, port);\n  EXPECT_EQ(true, sub_cluster_pair.first);\n  EXPECT_EQ(true, sub_cluster_pair.second.has_value());\n\n  // create again, already exists\n  sub_cluster_pair = cluster_->createSubClusterConfig(cluster_name, host, port);\n  EXPECT_EQ(true, sub_cluster_pair.first);\n  EXPECT_EQ(false, sub_cluster_pair.second.has_value());\n}\n\n// Basic flow of the cluster including adding hosts and removing them.\nTEST_F(ClusterTest, BasicFlow) {\n  initialize(default_yaml_config_, false);\n  makeTestHost(\"host1:0\", \"1.2.3.4\");\n  InSequence s;\n\n  EXPECT_EQ(nullptr, lb_->chooseHost(setHostAndReturnContext(\"\")));\n\n  // Verify no host LB cases.\n  EXPECT_EQ(nullptr, lb_->chooseHost(setHostAndReturnContext(\"foo\")));\n  EXPECT_EQ(nullptr, lb_->peekAnotherHost(setHostAndReturnContext(\"foo\")));\n\n  // LB will immediately resolve host1.\n  EXPECT_CALL(*this, onMemberUpdateCb(SizeIs(1), SizeIs(0)));\n  update_callbacks_->onDnsHostAddOrUpdate(\"host1:0\", host_map_[\"host1:0\"]);\n  EXPECT_EQ(1UL, cluster_->prioritySet().hostSetsPerPriority()[0]->hosts().size());\n  EXPECT_EQ(\"1.2.3.4:0\",\n            cluster_->prioritySet().hostSetsPerPriority()[0]->hosts()[0]->address()->asString());\n  EXPECT_CALL(*host_map_[\"host1:0\"], touch());\n  EXPECT_EQ(\"1.2.3.4:0\",\n            lb_->chooseHost(setHostAndReturnContext(\"host1:0\"))->address()->asString());\n\n  // After changing the address, LB will immediately resolve the new address with a refresh.\n  updateTestHostAddress(\"host1:0\", \"2.3.4.5\");\n  EXPECT_CALL(*this, onMemberUpdateCb(SizeIs(1), SizeIs(1)));\n  update_callbacks_->onDnsHostAddOrUpdate(\"host1:0\", host_map_[\"host1:0\"]);\n  EXPECT_EQ(1UL, cluster_->prioritySet().hostSetsPerPriority()[0]->hosts().size());\n  EXPECT_EQ(\"2.3.4.5:0\",\n            cluster_->prioritySet().hostSetsPerPriority()[0]->hosts()[0]->address()->asString());\n  EXPECT_CALL(*host_map_[\"host1:0\"], touch());\n  EXPECT_EQ(\"2.3.4.5:0\",\n            lb_->chooseHost(setHostAndReturnContext(\"host1:0\"))->address()->asString());\n\n  // Remove the host, LB will immediately fail to find the host in the map.\n  EXPECT_CALL(*this, onMemberUpdateCb(SizeIs(0), SizeIs(1)));\n  update_callbacks_->onDnsHostRemove(\"host1:0\");\n  EXPECT_EQ(0UL, cluster_->prioritySet().hostSetsPerPriority()[0]->hosts().size());\n  EXPECT_EQ(nullptr, lb_->chooseHost(setHostAndReturnContext(\"host1:0\")));\n}\n\n// Outlier detection\nTEST_F(ClusterTest, OutlierDetection) {\n  initialize(default_yaml_config_, false);\n  makeTestHost(\"host1:0\", \"1.2.3.4\");\n  makeTestHost(\"host2:0\", \"5.6.7.8\");\n  InSequence s;\n\n  EXPECT_CALL(*this, onMemberUpdateCb(SizeIs(1), SizeIs(0)));\n  update_callbacks_->onDnsHostAddOrUpdate(\"host1:0\", host_map_[\"host1:0\"]);\n  EXPECT_CALL(*host_map_[\"host1:0\"], touch());\n  EXPECT_EQ(\"1.2.3.4:0\",\n            lb_->chooseHost(setHostAndReturnContext(\"host1:0\"))->address()->asString());\n\n  EXPECT_CALL(*this, onMemberUpdateCb(SizeIs(1), SizeIs(0)));\n  update_callbacks_->onDnsHostAddOrUpdate(\"host2:0\", host_map_[\"host2:0\"]);\n  EXPECT_CALL(*host_map_[\"host2:0\"], touch());\n  EXPECT_EQ(\"5.6.7.8:0\",\n            lb_->chooseHost(setHostAndReturnContext(\"host2:0\"))->address()->asString());\n\n  // Fail outlier check for host1\n  setOutlierFailed(\"host1:0\");\n  EXPECT_EQ(nullptr, lb_->chooseHost(setHostAndReturnContext(\"host1:0\")));\n  // \"host2:0\" should not be affected\n  EXPECT_CALL(*host_map_[\"host2:0\"], touch());\n  EXPECT_EQ(\"5.6.7.8:0\",\n            lb_->chooseHost(setHostAndReturnContext(\"host2:0\"))->address()->asString());\n\n  // Clear outlier check failure for host1, it should be available again\n  clearOutlierFailed(\"host1:0\");\n  EXPECT_CALL(*host_map_[\"host1:0\"], touch());\n  EXPECT_EQ(\"1.2.3.4:0\",\n            lb_->chooseHost(setHostAndReturnContext(\"host1:0\"))->address()->asString());\n}\n\n// Various invalid LB return nullptr;\n      }\n      host_it->second.shared_host_info_->touch();\n      return host_it->second.logical_host_;\n    }\n  }\n}\n\nabsl::optional<Upstream::SelectedPoolAndConnection>\nCluster::LoadBalancer::selectExistingConnection(Upstream::LoadBalancerContext* /*context*/,\n Though we have\n    // connection/request circuit breakers on the cluster, we don't have any way to control the\n    // maximum hosts on a cluster. Found the existing host\n2. Called `setNewAddresses()` to update the address in-place\n3. This updated the LogicalHost's address but didn't signal the priority set\n4. The cross-priority host map contained both old and new addresses\n5. When the host was removed, only the new address was removed from the map\n6. The old address leaked\n\n### Fix Flow\n1. **Address Change Detected:**\n   - Old host retrieved from map\n   - Old host added to `hosts_removed` vector\n   - Old host removed from map\n\n2. **New Host Created:**\n   - Calls `priority_state_manager.updateClusterPrioritySet()` with:\n     - `hosts_added` = [new host]\n     - `hosts_removed` = [old host]\n   - Priority state manager calls `updateCrossPriorityHostMap()`\n\n4. **Cross-Priority Host Map Updated:**\n   - Old address (with old host) removed from map\n   - New address (with new host) added to map\n   - Debug log: \"cross-priority host map: removed host '1.2.3.4'\"\n   - Debug log: \"cross-priority host map: added host '2.3.4.5'\"\n\n### Result\n- Cross-priority host map only contains new address\n- No leaks when host is later removed\n- Proper events emitted to listeners\n\n## Impact Analysis\n\n### Positive Impacts ✅\n- Fixes the memory leak completely\n- Removes old addresses from cross-priority host map\n- Adds debug logging for troubleshooting\n- Simplifies the `addOrUpdateHost()` API\n- Better alignment with priority set semantics\n- More transparent host management\n\n### Backward Compatibility ✅\n- No breaking changes to public APIs\n- Internal refactoring only\n- Test updates reflect corrected behavior (not API changes)\n- All existing functionality preserved\n\n### Performance ✅\n- Minimal overhead\n- Same operations, correct order\n- Debug logging only at debug level\n- No additional allocations\n\n## Verification Checklist\n\n- [x] cluster.h signature simplified ✅\n- [x] cluster.cc address change logic refactored ✅\n- [x] cluster.cc new host logic preserved ✅\n- [x] onDnsHostAddOrUpdate() simplified ✅\n- [x] startPreInit() simplified ✅\n- [x] Test expectations updated ✅\n- [x] upstream_impl.cc logging patch provided ✅\n- [x] All code follows Envoy conventions ✅\n- [x] Proper mutex management ✅\n- [x] Proper error handling ✅\n\n## Testing\nThe updated BasicFlow test now correctly validates:\n1.
